;SSMAP EDA edited by Ravenant: May-2012
;SSHIP edited by MagicCuboid (added Skadar ancillaries), VineFynn
;SSHIP later versions edited by Jurand of Cracow 2020-22

;---------------------------------------------------------------------
; General assumptions for modding ancillaries:
; - make as many as possible transferable - swapping between generals is a part of the game for the player.
; - they should have 2 major benefits net (eg. 3 positive and 1 negative) for the player to bother to pay attention.
; - negative ancillaries are not transferable. They should also come very rarely.
;
;---------------------------------------------------------------------
; Advice for coding:
;--- put the strictest conditions (ie. true very rarely) at the beginning of each trigger to save processing time.
;--- in the triggers it's better to use > than = (eg.: > 95 is better than = 100, or [ >4 <6 ] instead of [=5]).
;--- don't use (Chance 1) - use RandomPercent > 80 and Chance 5 or similar
;--- be aware that you cannot change this order:
;------  ExcludedAncillaries XYZ
;------  ExcludeCultures XYZ 
;---- (also: you can exlude only up to 3 ancillaries in this way)
;
;---------------------------------------------------------------------
; Plans for further modding: cleaning, checking and modifications planned:
;--- generic ancillaries review, including grouping them into classes.
;--- byzantine offices and relics - to be reviewed
;--- Provincial Titles: one would have to do an additional set of PTs for the Rus factions
;  - at the moment they get those for the Catholics
;  - perhaps only for a limited number of provinces - like 20, separate titles "rking_"

;---------------------------------------------------------------------
; Ideas other ancillaries:
; - Herolds - +Authority, only Catholic, maybe only with blood, after a historic event: reflect cultural developments and creation of such posts
; - Saxo Grammaticus (only for Danes, once a cathedral of Lund is built, historically early 13c.)
; - Veit Stoss - after last level of Marienkirche built
; - items: elixir (differnt effects for all three cultures!) 

;---------------------------------------------------------------------
; Ideas for Muslim ancillaries:
; - Faqih (pl Fuqaha'):  an islamic jurist, an expert in fiqh (Islamic jurisprudence and Islamic Law)
; - al-Kashgari map - only for the Turks
; - Muslim version of the Defender of the Faith (ancillary protector) - al-Nasir li-Din Allah (ar-Rahman III got it)

;---------------------------------------------------------------------

	WhenToTest CharacterTurnEndInSettlement
	Condition AgentType = assassin
		and RemainingMPPercentage > 95
		and SettlementBuildingExists >= farms4
		and TimeInRegion > 4
	AcquireAncillary pet_bloodhound chance 10

;------------------------------------------

	WhenToTest CharacterTurnEndInSettlement
	Condition IsGeneral
		and RemainingMPPercentage > 95
		and TimeInRegion > 4
		and RandomPercent > 80
	AcquireAncillary pet_guarddog chance 2

;==========================================================;
;====   ANCILLARIES from battles ==========================;
;==========================================================;
; use: PercentageBodyguardKilled
; GeneralNumKillsInBattle - counts fleeing guys. Should be replaced or used with a reason.
; NumEnemiesInBattle - don't use it, it's a source of crashes
; GeneralPrisonersRansomedCaptor - doesn't work in EDA.
; GeneralHPLostRatioinBattle - perhaps bad condition given that HP is always 1?

;------------------------------------------ 
Trigger runner_vnv_trigger 
 WhenToTest PostBattle 
 Condition BattleSuccess = crushing 
 and PercentageBodyguardKilled > 10 
 and PercentageEnemyKilled > 66  
 and GeneralFoughtInCombat
 and IsGeneral
 and WonBattle
 and not Routs
 
 AcquireAncillary runner chance 10 
 
;------------------------------------------

 WhenToTest PostBattle 
 Condition GeneralNumKillsInBattle > 8 
 and PercentageBodyguardKilled > 60  
 and GeneralFoughtInCombat
 and IsGeneral
 and WonBattle
 and not Routs
 
 AcquireAncillary veteran_warrior chance 25

 WhenToTest PostBattle 
 Condition PercentageBodyguardKilled > 60
 and GeneralFoughtInCombat
 and IsGeneral
 and WonBattle
 and not Routs
 
 AcquireAncillary shieldbearer chance 15

 and PercentageEnemyKilled > 66  
 and GeneralFoughtInCombat
 and IsGeneral
 and WonBattle
 and not Routs
 
 AcquireAncillary swordbearer chance 10

 and GeneralFoughtInCombat
 and IsGeneral

;===================================================================================         KNOWLEDGE
;====   KNOWLEDGE   ================================================== 
;---------- Doctor, Physician, Apothecary
;---------- Alchemist, Astrologer, Brilliant Inventor
;---------- Mathematician, Scribe, Librarian
;---------- Siege Engineer, Architect, Master Mason

; very low probabilities but cumulative and fire quite often (since generals stay in as governors)
; triggers for GBC library, university, alchemist lab, balistas are in the other sections

;   (A) Ancs increasing settlement growth and/or lowering casualties after battle:
; Doctor: staying with university or bimaristan (T4)
; Physician: from the battles with high casualties and healing wounds in-wilde
; Apothecary: from various educational buildings (T3/T4)
;   (B) Ancs with battle benefits
; Alchemist: staying with alchemist labs (T4)
; Astrologer: staying with university (T4), pagan sanctuaries (T4); difficult battles won;
; Siege Engineer: staying with siege buildings (C3, T3) and sieges won
;   (C) Ancs increasing income & other
; Mathematician: staying with university (T4)
; Scribe: staying with town halls (T2)
; Librarian: staying with libraries (T3)
;   (D) lowering costs of buildings
; Brilliant Inventor: staying with mines (C3,T3), alchemist lab (T4), university (T4), buildings finished (T4), and from patronage (anc Office, Crown)
; Architect: buildings finished if university exists; big buildings finished
; Master Mason: staying with masons guilds (C3), building masons guilds, patronage (anc Office)
;
; (0) Cross-sectional triggers for 6 university related ancs: Scholar+University, Everybody+GreatUniversity
;
; special easy triggers for the AI have not been yet added

;------------------------------------------------------------------------- ALL

;------------------------------------------ University (T4) All for Scholars 1%
Trigger Academics_Staying_University_Scholar_NoXenophobia
 WhenToTest CharacterTurnEndInSettlement
 
 Condition RandomPercent > 80
 and RemainingMPPercentage > 95
 and SettlementBuildingExists >= university
 and Trait Xenophobia < 1 
 and Trait Wantschool < 1 
 and Trait WantsHigherEd > 0 
 and not IsFactionLeader 
 and not IsUnderSiege

 AcquireAncillary apothecary chance 5
 AcquireAncillary alchemist chance 5 
 AcquireAncillary librarian chance 5 
 AcquireAncillary mathematician chance 5  
 AcquireAncillary doctor chance 5
 AcquireAncillary astrologer chance 5 
 
;------------------------------------------ GreatUniversity (T5) All for All 1%
Trigger Academics_Staying_GreatLibrary_NoXenophobia
 WhenToTest CharacterTurnEndInSettlement
 
 Condition RandomPercent > 80
 and RemainingMPPercentage > 95
 and SettlementBuildingExists > university
 and Trait Wantschool < 1 
 and Trait Xenophobia < 1 
 and not IsFactionLeader 
 and IsGeneral
 and not IsUnderSiege
 
 AcquireAncillary apothecary chance 5
 AcquireAncillary alchemist chance 5 
 AcquireAncillary librarian chance 5 
 AcquireAncillary doctor chance 5
 AcquireAncillary astrologer chance 5

 and IsGeneral
 and not IsUnderSiege
 
 AcquireAncillary librarian chance 5

;====   EDUCATION   ========================================================= Education
;
; Mentor for the martial matters, Tutor & AcadAdv for the civilian
; all are mutually excluded (a general can have only 1)
; Mentor and Tutor received at CoA thanks to Father&Mother traits
; Academic Advisor received during education at university due to own traits

; possible modification in the future:
; - make them all transferable (enables setting the orders of ancillaries on a general, good for the experience)
; - make them very rare: very low probability of getting, this would be a valuable asset passed from a youngster to another


;---------- Mentor ------------------------------------------------- mentor

;------------------------------------------
Trigger Mentor_Father_Military
 WhenToTest CharacterComesOfAge 
 
 Condition FatherTrait MilitaryInclination > 0
	and Trait MilitaryInclination > 0 
	
 AcquireAncillary mentor chance 10
 
;------------------------------------------ 
Trigger Mentor_Father_AuthorityHigh
 WhenToTest CharacterComesOfAge 

 Condition FatherAttribute Authority > 6
	and Trait MilitaryInclination > 0 
	
 AcquireAncillary mentor chance 10

;------------------------------------------

 WhenToTest CharacterComesOfAge 

 Condition FatherAttribute Authority > 3
	and Trait MilitaryInclination > 0 
	
 AcquireAncillary mentor chance 10

;------------------------------------------

 WhenToTest CharacterComesOfAge 

 Condition FatherAttribute Command > 6
	and Trait MilitaryInclination > 0 
	
 AcquireAncillary mentor chance 10

;------------------------------------------

 WhenToTest CharacterComesOfAge 

 Condition FatherAttribute Chivalry > 6
	and Trait MilitaryInclination > 0 
	
 AcquireAncillary mentor chance 10

;------------------------------------------ 
Trigger Mentor_Father_DreadHigh
 WhenToTest CharacterComesOfAge 

 Condition FatherAttribute Chivalry < -6
	and Trait MilitaryInclination > 0 
	
 AcquireAncillary mentor chance 10
  
;------------------------------------------ 
Trigger Mentor_Father_Intelligent
 WhenToTest CharacterComesOfAge 

 Condition FatherTrait Intelligent > 6
	and Trait MilitaryInclination > 0 
	
 AcquireAncillary mentor chance 10

	and Trait MilitaryInclination > 0

	Condition SettlementBuildingFinished = artist_studio

		and RemainingMPPercentage > 95
		and SettlementBuildingExists >= theatre
	AcquireAncillary musician chance 3

	WhenToTest CharacterTurnEndInSettlement

		and RemainingMPPercentage > 95
		and SettlementBuildingExists >= fairground
		and RandomPercent > 50
	AcquireAncillary musician chance 5

	WhenToTest CharacterTurnEndInSettlement
	Condition IsGeneral
		and RemainingMPPercentage > 95
		and SettlementBuildingExists >= jousting_lists
		and RandomPercent > 80
	AcquireAncillary musician chance 5

;------------------------------------------

		and RandomPercent > 50

		and SettlementBuildingExists >= tavern

;========================================================================================
;====   BOOKS   =========================================================================
;========================================================================================
;- all books are transferable, one general can have many books but only one of each type (not really a problem as there's often only one book type per religion)
;- all books can be found (1%) in Great Libraries (T5) by a intelligent (>5) general with the relevant inclination (given the number of books available it makes ca. 5% chance to get any book)
;- otherwise they're found by Scholars (1%) in libraries (T3 or C3) with the relevant building present (usually T4, eg. Cathedral for Religion books)
;- some books may be acquired after a conquest of a great city or a city that was historically related to that book
;- poetry books are acquired only with Chivalry 3 - from libraries, for catholics also from Jousting Lists and castle libraries
;- three Italian poetry books come after 1300 and require only libraries; also one Turkish book comes late
;- usually there's no need to put conditions " and not HasAncType x" because books of the same type are excluded in the definitions


;=========================================================================== BOOKS FOR AI
;---------- Books AI Boost --------------------------------

;---------------------------------------------------------- catholic
;------------------------------------------
Trigger books_milit_AI_catholic
 WhenToTest CharacterTurnEndInSettlement 

 Condition not FactionIsLocal 
 and SettlementBuildingExists >= library 
 and FactionReligion catholic
 and Trait Intelligent > 4
 and Trait MilitaryInclination > 0 

 AcquireAncillary bookmilit_vegetius chance 5 
 AcquireAncillary bookgeogr_peutinger chance 5 
 AcquireAncillary bookhistor_vitacarolimagni chance 5 
 AcquireAncillary bookpoet_miocid chance 5 
 AcquireAncillary bookpoet_minnensang chance 5 
 
;------------------------------------------
Trigger books_admin_AI_catholic
 WhenToTest CharacterTurnEndInSettlement 

 Condition not FactionIsLocal 
 and SettlementBuildingExists >= library 
 and FactionReligion catholic 
 and Trait Intelligent > 4
 and Trait GovernorInclination > 0 
 
 AcquireAncillary booklegal_codexiustinianus chance 5

 WhenToTest CharacterTurnEndInSettlement 

 Condition RandomPercent > 80 
 and Trait WantsHigherEd > 0 
 and RemainingMPPercentage > 95 
 and SettlementBuildingExists >= library 
 and SettlementBuildingExists >= landowners4 
 and FactionReligion catholic
 and not IsUnderSiege
 
 AcquireAncillary bookmilit_vegetius chance 5 

;------------------------------------------ remember: MilMind generals cannot be scholar

 WhenToTest CharacterTurnEndInSettlement 

 Condition RandomPercent > 80
 and RemainingMPPercentage > 95 
 and SettlementBuildingExists >= castle_library 
 and Trait Intelligent > 5
 and Trait MilitaryInclination > 0
 and not IsUnderSiege
 
 AcquireAncillary bookmilit_vegetius chance 5

 WhenToTest CharacterTurnEndInSettlement

 and Trait WantsHigherEd > 0 
 and RemainingMPPercentage > 95 
 and SettlementBuildingExists >= library 
 and SettlementBuildingExists >= landowners4 
 and FactionReligion orthodox
 and not IsUnderSiege
 
 AcquireAncillary bookmilit_strategikon chance 5

 WhenToTest CharacterTurnEndInSettlement

;=================================================================================== CRUSADER KNIGHTS 
;---------- Crusader Knights ------------------------------
; IsOnCrusade - Test is character on crusade
; IsCrusade - It's true for crusade and false for jihad

;------------------------------------------------------ from battles
Trigger Crusade_Santiago_Battle_Leon
 WhenToTest PostBattle 
 
 Condition IsOnCrusade
 and WasAttacker
 and WonBattle 
 and IsGeneral 
 and BattleOdds >= 0.5 
 and BattleOdds < 1.5 
 and FactionType spain
 
 AcquireAncillary knight_santiago chance 40 
 
;------------------------------------------ 
Trigger Crusade_Santiago_Battle_Portugal
 WhenToTest PostBattle 
 
 Condition IsOnCrusade
 and WasAttacker
 and WonBattle 
 and IsGeneral 
 and BattleOdds >= 0.5 
 and BattleOdds < 1.5 
 and FactionType portugal
 
 AcquireAncillary knight_santiago chance 40 
 
;------------------------------------------ 
Trigger Crusade_Santiago_Battle_Aragon 
 WhenToTest PostBattle 
 
 Condition IsOnCrusade
 and WasAttacker

;---------- Horses ----------------------------------------

;------------------------------------------ Command 3+, MilMind, earls_stables, Castle: 4%
Trigger Trusty_Steed_earls_stables
 WhenToTest CharacterTurnEndInSettlement 
 
 Condition RemainingMPPercentage > 95 
	and SettlementBuildingExists >= earls_stables 
	and TimeInRegion > 4
	and Trait GoodCavalryGeneral >= 1 
	and Trait MilitaryInclination > 0
	and not HasAncType Steed 
	and Attribute Command > 2 
	and RandomPercent > 80

 AcquireAncillary trusty_steed chance 20 

;------------------------------------------

 WhenToTest CharacterTurnEndInSettlement
 Condition IsGeneral
 and RemainingMPPercentage > 95 
 and SettlementBuildingExists >= knights_stables 
 and not HasAncType Steed 
 and Attribute Command > 3 
 and Treasury > 15000 
 
 AcquireAncillary black_stallion chance 15 
 
;------------------------------------------

 WhenToTest CharacterTurnEndInSettlement
 Condition IsGeneral
 and RemainingMPPercentage > 95 
 and SettlementBuildingExists >= knights_stables 
 and not HasAncType Steed 
 and Attribute Command > 3 
 and Treasury > 15000 
 
 AcquireAncillary white_stallion chance 15

;=================================================================================== Armour 
;---------- Armour ----------------------------------------
;
; Strong Armour (Regular) - only 1HP, military generals Comm +3, after sitting with Armourer for some time
; Fitted Armour (Custom) - 2HP, military generals Comm +5 with special traits or MasterSmith or at events
; Ornate Armour (Ornate) - -1HP but +1 Auth +1 Popular: generals in cities or as marriage gift
; buildings built: MasterSmith or Armour Regular
; there's a window describing the system shown to the player as a historical event

;---------------------------------------------------------- ARMOUR REGULAR
;------------- Armour Regular -----------------------------

;------------------------------------------ Command 3+, MilMind, Armourer, Castle: 2%
Trigger Armour_Regular_Castle 
 WhenToTest CharacterTurnEndInSettlement 
 
 Condition RemainingMPPercentage > 95 
	and SettlementBuildingExists >= c_armourer 
	and TimeInRegion > 4
	and Trait MilitaryInclination > 0
	and Attribute Command > 2 
	and RandomPercent > 80
 
 AcquireAncillary armour_regular chance 10 

;------------------------------------------ Command 3+, MilMind, Armourer, City: 2%
Trigger Armour_Regular_City
 WhenToTest CharacterTurnEndInSettlement 
 
 Condition RemainingMPPercentage > 95 
	and SettlementBuildingExists >= armourer 
	and TimeInRegion > 4
	and Trait MilitaryInclination > 0
	and Attribute Command > 2 
	and RandomPercent > 80
 
 AcquireAncillary armour_regular chance 10 

;------------------------------------------ Command 3+, PostBattle: 1%
Trigger Armour_Regular_PostBattle 
 WhenToTest PostBattle 
 
 Condition Attribute Command > 2 
	and WonBattle 
	and BattleOdds > 1.0 
	and GeneralFoughtInCombat 
	and RandomPercent > 80
 
 AcquireAncillary armour_regular chance 5
 

;---------------------------------------------------------- ARMOUR CUSTOM
;------------- Armour Custom ------------------------------ 
 
;------------------------------------------ Command 5+, Armourer, Castle: 4%
Trigger Armour_Custom_Castle 
 WhenToTest CharacterTurnEndInSettlement 
 
 Condition RemainingMPPercentage > 95 
	and SettlementBuildingExists >= c_armourer 
	and Trait MilitaryInclination > 0
	and Attribute Command > 4 
	and RandomPercent > 80
 
 AcquireAncillary armour_custom chance 20 

;------------------------------------------ Command 5+, Guild: 2%
Trigger Armour_Custom_swordsmiths_guild 
 WhenToTest CharacterTurnEndInSettlement 
 
 Condition RemainingMPPercentage > 95 
	and SettlementBuildingExists >= swordsmiths_guild 
	and Trait MilitaryInclination > 0
	and Attribute Command > 4
	and RandomPercent > 80
 
 AcquireAncillary armour_custom chance 10 

;------------------------------------------ Paranoia, Armourer, City: 2%
Trigger Armour_Custom_City_Paranoia 
 WhenToTest CharacterTurnEndInSettlement 
 
 Condition RemainingMPPercentage > 95 
	and SettlementBuildingExists >= armourer 
	and Trait MilitaryInclination > 0
	and Trait Paranoia > 0
	and RandomPercent > 80
 
 AcquireAncillary armour_custom chance 10 

;------------------------------------------ Command 3+, Armourer, Castle, Military Minister visiting: 4%
Trigger Armour_Custom_Castle_Minister
 WhenToTest CharacterTurnEndInSettlement 
 
 Condition Attribute Command > 2
	and SettlementBuildingExists >= c_armourer 
	and Trait MilitaryInclination > 0    ; to distinguish military offices from non-military
	and HasAncType office
	and RandomPercent > 80
 
 AcquireAncillary armour_custom chance 20 

;------------------------------------------ Anc MasterSmiths, City: 1%
Trigger Armour_Custom_City_MasterSmith
 WhenToTest CharacterTurnEndInSettlement 
 
 Condition RemainingMPPercentage > 95 
	and SettlementBuildingExists >= armourer
	and HasAncType MasterSmith 
	and RandomPercent > 80
 
 AcquireAncillary armour_custom chance 5 
 
;------------------------------------------ Anc MasterSmiths, Castle: 1%
Trigger Armour_Custom_Castle_MasterSmith
 WhenToTest CharacterTurnEndInSettlement 
 
 Condition RemainingMPPercentage > 95 
	and SettlementBuildingExists >= c_armourer
	and HasAncType MasterSmith 
	and RandomPercent > 80
 
 AcquireAncillary armour_custom chance 5
 
;------------------------------------------ Command 3+, JoinCrusade: 10%
Trigger Armour_Custom_Crusade 
 WhenToTest GeneralJoinCrusade 
 
 Condition Attribute Command > 2 
	and RandomPercent > 80
 
 AcquireAncillary armour_custom chance 50 

;------------------------------------------ Command 3+, PostBattle: 2%
Trigger Armour_Custom_PostBattle 
 WhenToTest PostBattle 
 
 Condition Attribute Command > 2 
	and WonBattle 
	and BattleOdds < 0.8 
	and GeneralFoughtInCombat 
	and RandomPercent > 80
 
 AcquireAncillary armour_custom chance 10

;------- BOOK OF KELLS --------------------- Pious Capturing Dublin 50% 
Trigger book_of_kells_Capture
 WhenToTest GeneralCaptureSettlement 

 Condition Attribute Piety > 2 
 and SettlementName Dublin 
 and not I_WorldwideAncillaryExists relic_bookofkells 
 and not HasAncType Relic 

 AcquireAncillary relic_bookofkells chance 50

;------------------------------------------ Very Pious Scholar Staying 2%
Trigger book_of_kells_Studying
 WhenToTest GeneralCaptureSettlement 

 Condition Attribute Piety > 5 
 and SettlementName Dublin 
 and Trait Wantschool < 1
 and Trait WantsHigherEd > 0
 and not I_WorldwideAncillaryExists relic_bookofkells 
 and not HasAncType Relic 
 and RandomPercent > 80

 AcquireAncillary relic_bookofkells chance 10

;==========================================================;
;------- CHAMBERLAIN ----------------------
;------------------------------------------ 
Trigger chamberlain_europe_player
  WhenToTest CharacterTurnEndInSettlement
 Condition IsFactionLeader
 and FactionIsLocal
 and Trait FitForOffice > 1
 and not HasAncType office
 and not FactionwideAncillaryExists chamberlain
 and SettlementBuildingExists >= coaching_house  
 and I_TurnNumber > 50

  AcquireAncillary chamberlain chance 100

;------------------------------------------ 
Trigger chamberlain_greek_player
  WhenToTest CharacterTurnEndInSettlement
 Condition IsFactionLeader
 and FactionIsLocal
 and Trait FitForOffice > 1
 and not HasAncType office
 and not FactionwideAncillaryExists chamberlain_greek
 and SettlementBuildingExists >= coaching_house  
 and I_TurnNumber > 50
 
  AcquireAncillary chamberlain_greek chance 100
  
;------------------------------------------

  WhenToTest CharacterTurnEndInSettlement
 Condition IsFactionLeader
 and FactionIsLocal
 and Trait FitForOffice > 1
 and not HasAncType office
 and not FactionwideAncillaryExists chamberlain_muslim
 and SettlementBuildingExists >= coaching_house  
 and I_TurnNumber > 50
 
   AcquireAncillary chamberlain_muslim chance 100

 and not IsFactionHeir

 and SettlementBuildingExists >= tavern    
 and not FactionwideAncillaryExists chamberlain
 
 AcquireAncillary chamberlain chance 50

 and not FactionIsLocal

 and not FactionwideAncillaryExists moh_muslim
 and not HasAncType office
 
 AcquireAncillary moh_muslim chance 50

Trigger banner_of_Great_Constantine
 WhenToTest CharacterTurnEndInSettlement
 Condition IsFactionLeader
 and SettlementName Constantinople
 and FactionType byzantium 
 and Trait FitForOffice > 1
 and not I_WorldwideAncillaryExists banner_of_Great_Constantine
 and not HasAncType Relic_banner
 and Trait GoodCommander >= 3

 AcquireAncillary banner_of_Great_Constantine chance 33
;----------------------------------------------
Trigger sword_of_Basil_Bulgaroctonos
 WhenToTest CharacterTurnEndInSettlement
 Condition IsGeneral
 and SettlementName Tarnovo
 and FactionType byzantium 
 and Trait FitForOffice > 1
 and not I_WorldwideAncillaryExists sword_of_Basil_Bulgaroctonos
 and not HasAncType Relic_sword
 and Trait GoodCommander >= 3

 AcquireAncillary sword_of_Basil_Bulgaroctonos chance 33
;----------------------------------------------
Trigger Banner_of_Herakleios
 WhenToTest PostBattle
 Condition WonBattle
 and FactionReligion catholic
 and GeneralFoughtCulture middle_eastern
 and BattleSuccess = crushing
 and FactionType byzantium 
 and not I_WorldwideAncillaryExists Banner_of_Herakleios
 and not HasAncType Relic_banner
 and Trait GoodCommander >= 3
 
 AcquireAncillary Banner_of_Herakleios chance 66
;----------------------------------------------
Trigger sword_of_Great_Constantine
 WhenToTest PostBattle
 Condition IsGeneral
 and WonBattle
 and PercentageEnemyKilled > 25
 and BattleOdds <= 0.50
 and FactionType byzantium 
 and not I_WorldwideAncillaryExists sword_of_Great_Constantine
 and not HasAncType Relic_sword
 and Trait GoodCommander >= 3

 AcquireAncillary sword_of_Great_Constantine chance 66
;----------------------------------------------
